NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
R. Suresh Valliappan alias C. Alagiyameiappan, Natural son of A.T. Rajendran, residing at New No. 8/1, Ramaswamy
Muthaliyar Street, Kochadai, Madurai-625 016, by way of this Public Notice, I inform, that (late) Shri. S. Chinnakaruppan
Chettiyar, has legally adopted me as his son on 26th May 2003 by way a Registered Deed No. 91 of 2003, on the file of
the Sub-Registrar of Thiruppathur. My Adopted Father Shri. S. Chinnakaruppan Chettiyar passed away
on 31st May 2003. Hereafter I shall be known as C. ALAGIYAMEIAPPAN.

Madurai, 5th July 2011.

R. SURESH VALLIAPPAN alias
C. ALAGIYAMEIAPPAN.

PRINTED AND PUBLISHED BY THE DIRECTOR OF STATIONERY AND PRINTING, CHENNAI
ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
